	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "意識を、失った。",
			NULL, "Tomoe lost consciousness.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DrawScene("background/m_y4_07", 250 );
	ModDrawCharacter(4, 2, "sprite/night/re4_hig_def_a1_", "0", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 19, 100, TRUE );
	PlaySE(3, "down3", 256, 64);
	ShakeScreen( 1, 15, 15, 2, 0, );
	Wait( 250 );
	Negative( 500, TRUE );

//レナrvS11/02/420700037.「あははははははは、あはははははははははははっっ！！！」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#f0953d>レナ</color>", NULL, "<color=#f0953d>Rena</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 2, "ps3/s11/02/420700037", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「あははははははは、あはははははははははははっっ！！！」",
			NULL, "\"Ahahahahahahaha, ahahahahahahahahahahahah!!!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	FadeFilm( 1500, FALSE );

	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 3000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 1300, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	DrawBustshot(6, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene( "black", 3000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

}
